  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_b759ba44-6a90-4c06-b571-b6ac1ae515b8'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }
  //]]>

<span id="freeTextContainer10528883016951955082">Bestowed is the story of Rudra and Arya. A story of friendship, love, betrayal, and obsession. Rudra, a stranger Arya didn't remember meeting; but he knew more about her than she did about herself. Who was this stranger? Why did he seem so familiar? Why was she attracted to him? From the day he visited Arya’s house, Rudra had wanted to take her in his arms and tell her eve</span>
  <span id="freeText10528883016951955082" style="display:none">Bestowed is the story of Rudra and Arya. A story of friendship, love, betrayal, and obsession. Rudra, a stranger Arya didn't remember meeting; but he knew more about her than she did about herself. Who was this stranger? Why did he seem so familiar? Why was she attracted to him? From the day he visited Arya’s house, Rudra had wanted to take her in his arms and tell her everything. But, he refrained himself and decided to wait for her to remember... and recognize him. Will she remember him... or will he have to lose her once again. 'Bestowed' - A saga of love!<br /><br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://notionpress.com/read/bestowed">https://notionpress.com/read/bestowed</a></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span> (Review from the author)


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/102565864-snehlata-agarwala?shelf=young-adults">young-adults</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3005145825" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2003175854579300075">I know I am the author and I am not entitled to review my own book. But still, I will.<br/>I stated this story just as a chapter in a fb group. And then it kept on building in my mind.<br/>As I wrote this, I fell in love with "Rudra" who as his name states is committed and focused. And a girl, Arya, who is sweet, and had been through a lot in her life. <br/><br/>The Bengali culture is something I have been brought up in, so it is more dear to me than my own marwari culture and you will get a glimpse of my love for </span>
  <span id="freeText2003175854579300075" style="display:none">I know I am the author and I am not entitled to review my own book. But still, I will.<br />I stated this story just as a chapter in a fb group. And then it kept on building in my mind.<br />As I wrote this, I fell in love with "Rudra" who as his name states is committed and focused. And a girl, Arya, who is sweet, and had been through a lot in her life. <br /><br />The Bengali culture is something I have been brought up in, so it is more dear to me than my own marwari culture and you will get a glimpse of my love for it in the story.<br /><br />This was my first story, and I hope I was able to do justice to it.<br /><br />And it is a story of eternal love, because love is always selfless and beautiful. And love always finds it's way. &lt;3 <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="2003175854579300075" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>


      <div class="reviewFooter uitext buttons">

  <span id="freeText1586177485626547767" style="display:none">Okay okay, let me be calm before writing this review. For the story, you can check the book's blurb in the description, I don't want to bore you. So let me get straight into my review.<br /><br />Before writing, what I liked about this book, let me tell you what I disliked in this book. Ummmm, there is not a single thing that I can point about disliking this book. This book is definitely one of the best books that I have ever read.<br /><br />The story is all about the love between Arya and Rudra, and their eternal love. Can you believe Rudra waited for 10 long years to get back his love again? <br /><br />Though the book has some side plots mainly the story revolves around Arya and Rudra. The author has done a commendable job by simultaneously narrating the stories from the past and present. Not for a single time, I was able to drop the book before completely reading it.<br /><br />Definitely, this book is a page-turner and one can never stop without completing it. Though it ended I craved for more. I was so engrossed in the book that I didn't realize how the time flew by. <br /><br />If you are looking for some Romance genre books and quite new to the world of books, then don't think twice before picking it up. Trust me you won't regret reading this book. <br /><br />Don't remember the last time I had read such a lovely book.</span>

  <span id="freeText18446629527634999574" style="display:none">Let me begin with stating a few words about the story. It is a story of two people so much in love that the universe tries to bring them together in spite of all the barriers and hardships they have faced. Rudra and Arya are the two protagonists of the story who have a magnetic bond attracting them towards each other. The story has been woven together with a Bengali backdrop. The smallest of details that represent Bengali culture has been distinctly stated in the book which paints a picture of the story in front of your eyes. You can imagine the scenes playing before you, which is a huge accomplishment as a writer. <br />The story as a whole is light and heart-warming. I couldn't keep it aside until it was over. It's a must read for all those who yearn for a beautiful love story.</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('kBAeMjIckIb9+sQXaA6eGZh4NrH1D7EGhsmaU9YWpAYJ2EoaGidiLIhei66Otu7UvjRg5DsO1tkU03CGKwMYUA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('X1xZDoT8G3LqTmjVxWNiZz74loIPi+BndU4qkcIbbhjGlA0mrMfp2J/qJ2wj2xKqGLTA18GKh7jnVMBEPw7STg==')})
  }
